### Shared Focuses ###
shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_black_monday
	icon = GFX_goal_HOL_black_monday
	x = 0
	y = 0
	
	
	cost = 4
	available = { has_idea = rus_black_monday }
	bypass = {
		has_idea = rus_black_monday
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_idea = RUS_civil_war_aftermath_idea
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
	add_political_power = 25
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_taxes
	icon = GFX_goal_CZE_income_tax
	cost = 4
	prerequisite = { focus = RUS_Senate_Plan }
	relative_position_id = RUS_black_monday
	x = 3
	y = 2
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
	}
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_KER
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = russia_must_wait_unlock
				has_country_flag = unlock_economy
			}
		}
	}
	bypass = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_idea = RUS_civil_war_aftermath_idea
		}
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		add_political_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_1
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_1
				add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_3
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = rus_black_monday
				add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_2
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { 
					id = russia.25 
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}		
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_Balance_The_Budget
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_financial_markets
	cost = 3 
	prerequisite = { 
		focus = RUS_Ease_The_Peasant_Burden
		focus = RUS_Encourage_Private_Investment
	}
	prerequisite = { 
		focus = RUS_Economy_Under_State_Control
		focus = RUS_Encourage_Private_Investment
	}
	
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_KER
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = russia_must_wait_unlock
				has_country_flag = unlock_economy
			}
		}
	}
	bypass = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_idea = RUS_civil_war_aftermath_idea
		}
	}
	
	relative_position_id = RUS_black_monday
	x = 0
	y = 4
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Duma_Plan
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_4
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Senate_Plan
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_4
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_5
				}
			}
		}
		else = {		
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_Balance_The_Budget_tooltip
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_4
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_5
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_4
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_5
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = russia.26 days = 180 }
		}
	}
}
shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_Reinstitute_The_Zemstva
	icon = GFX_BRY_Power_To_Zemstva
	relative_position_id = RUS_Balance_The_Budget
	x = -3
	y = 1
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = {
		focus = RUS_Balance_The_Budget
	}
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = RUS_economy_is_unlocked
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_4
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_5						
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_6
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_4
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_5
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_6
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_right_democratic_government = yes
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
			has_country_flag = RUS_PUR
			AND = {
				is_subject = yes
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Lavr Kornilov"
				}
			}
			has_completed_focus = RUS_kornilov_ruler
		}
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = RUS_Bureaucratic_Overhaul
		focus = RUS_Restructure_Economy
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 25
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_Reinstitute_The_Zemstva"
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_ideas = RUS_new_zemstva_1
		RUS_reduce_german_influence = yes
	}
}

	}

shared_focus = { 
	id = RUS_Local_Development
	icon = GFX_goal_NFA_Work_With_Local_Businesses
	relative_position_id = RUS_Reinstitute_The_Zemstva
	x = -1
	y = 2
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = {
		focus = RUS_Funding_Frenzy
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 60
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_Local_Development"
		add_stability = 0.06
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 651 decision = RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State } #Ufa
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 248 decision = RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State } #Yaroslavl
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 252 decision = RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State } #Nizhny Novgorod
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 250 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 224 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_Local_Development_tooltip
		if = { #has investment bank
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_6 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_6
				add_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_7
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_1
				add_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_2
			}
		}
	}
}
shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_Zemstvo_Research_Initiatives
	icon = GFX_goal_military_research
	relative_position_id = RUS_Reinstitute_The_Zemstva
	x = -2
	y = 3
	cost = 8
	prerequisite = {
		focus = RUS_Local_Development
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 60
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_Zemstvo_Research_Initiatives"
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_Zemstvo_Research_Initiatives_tooltip
		add_research_slot = 1
		if = { #has war preparations
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_4 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_4
				add_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_5
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has investment bank
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_7 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_7
				add_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_8
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has war preparations and investment bank
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_9 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_9
				add_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_10
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_2
				add_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_3
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_Restructure_Economy
	icon = GFX_focus_SOV_merge_plants
	relative_position_id = RUS_Balance_The_Budget
	x = 0
	y = 1
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = {
		focus = RUS_Balance_The_Budget
	}
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = RUS_economy_is_unlocked
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_4
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_5						
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_6
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_4
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_5
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_6
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_right_democratic_government = no
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_country_flag = RUS_PUR
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_subject = yes
				has_authoritarian_government = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = RUS_Bureaucratic_Overhaul
		focus = RUS_Reinstitute_The_Zemstva
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 25
	}
	completion_reward = {
		add_stability = 0.06
		add_research_slot = 1
		RUS_reduce_german_influence = yes
	}
}

		}

				psr_in_power = yes
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Alexandr Kerensky"

					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_The_Land_Quotas_Bill
				has_completed_focus = RUS_soc_land
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				rsdrp_in_power = yes 
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_vi_congress_moderates
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_vi_congress_internationalists
					has_country_flag = RUS_decided_to_stay_democratic
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = nsp_in_power
					has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_I_Bukharin_hog_syn
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Future_Of_The_Republic_2
				has_country_flag = RUS_decided_to_stay_democratic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_vi_congress_internationalists
				rsdrp_in_power = yes	
			}
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Future_Of_The_Republic_mensh_2
				has_country_flag = RUS_decided_to_stay_democratic
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = lpsr_not_in_power
			NOT = { has_idea = RUS_Vladimir_K_Volsky_hog_rso }
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = plsr_not_in_power
			NOT = { has_idea = RUS_Maria_A_Spiridonova_hog_rso }
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
